- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Selects execution host strategy for shell commands, typically controlling local vs delegated execution environment. Use the safest host mode that still satisfies your automation requirements.

### `tools.exec.node`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Node binding configuration for exec tooling when command execution is delegated through connected nodes. Use explicit node binding only when multi-node routing is required.

### `tools.exec.notifyOnExit`

- Type: `boolean`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: When true (default), backgrounded exec sessions on exit and node exec lifecycle events enqueue a system event and request a heartbeat.

### `tools.exec.notifyOnExitEmptySuccess`

- Type: `boolean`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: When true, successful backgrounded exec exits with empty output still enqueue a completion system event (default: false).

- Default: _none_

## UI

UI presentation settings for accenting and assistant identity shown in control surfaces. Use this for branding and readability customization without changing runtime behavior.

### `ui`

- Type: `object`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: UI presentation settings for accenting and assistant identity shown in control surfaces. Use this for branding and readability customization without changing runtime behavior.

### `ui.assistant`

- Type: `object`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Assistant display identity settings for name and avatar shown in UI surfaces. Keep these values aligned with your operator-facing persona and support expectations.

### `ui.assistant.avatar`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Assistant avatar image source used in UI surfaces (URL, path, or data URI depending on runtime support). Use trusted assets and consistent branding dimensions for clean rendering.

### `ui.assistant.name`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Display name shown for the assistant in UI views, chat chrome, and status contexts. Keep this stable so operators can reliably identify which assistant persona is active.

### `ui.seamColor`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Primary accent/seam color used by UI surfaces for emphasis, badges, and visual identity cues. Use high-contrast values that remain readable across light/dark themes.

## Updates

Update-channel and startup-check behavior for keeping OpenClaw runtime versions current. Use conservative channels in production and more experimental channels only in controlled environments.

### `update`

- Type: `object`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Update-channel and startup-check behavior for keeping OpenClaw runtime versions current. Use conservative channels in production and more experimental channels only in controlled environments.

### `update.auto`

- Type: `object`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: _No description provided._

### `update.auto.betaCheckIntervalHours`

- Type: `number`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: How often beta-channel checks run in hours (default: 1).

### `update.auto.enabled`

- Type: `boolean`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Enable background auto-update for package installs (default: false).

### `update.auto.stableDelayHours`

- Type: `number`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Minimum delay before stable-channel auto-apply starts (default: 6).

### `update.auto.stableJitterHours`

- Type: `number`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Extra stable-channel rollout spread window in hours (default: 12).

### `update.channel`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Update channel for git + npm installs ("stable", "beta", or "dev").

### `update.checkOnStart`

- Type: `boolean`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Check for npm updates when the gateway starts (default: true).

## Web Channel

Web channel runtime settings for heartbeat and reconnect behavior when operating web-based chat surfaces. Use reconnect values tuned to your network reliability profile and expected uptime needs.

### `web`

- Type: `object`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Web channel runtime settings for heartbeat and reconnect behavior when operating web-based chat surfaces. Use reconnect values tuned to your network reliability profile and expected uptime needs.

### `web.enabled`

- Type: `boolean`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Enables the web channel runtime and related websocket lifecycle behavior. Keep disabled when web chat is unused to reduce active connection management overhead.

### `web.heartbeatSeconds`

- Type: `integer`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Heartbeat interval in seconds for web channel connectivity and liveness maintenance. Use shorter intervals for faster detection, or longer intervals to reduce keepalive chatter.

### `web.reconnect`

- Type: `object`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Reconnect backoff policy for web channel reconnect attempts after transport failure. Keep bounded retries and jitter tuned to avoid thundering-herd reconnect behavior.

### `web.reconnect.factor`

- Type: `number`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Exponential backoff multiplier used between reconnect attempts in web channel retry loops. Keep factor above 1 and tune with jitter for stable large-fleet reconnect behavior.

### `web.reconnect.initialMs`

- Type: `number`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Initial reconnect delay in milliseconds before the first retry after disconnection. Use modest delays to recover quickly without immediate retry storms.

### `web.reconnect.jitter`

- Type: `number`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Randomization factor (0-1) applied to reconnect delays to desynchronize clients after outage events. Keep non-zero jitter in multi-client deployments to reduce synchronized spikes.

### `web.reconnect.maxAttempts`

- Type: `integer`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Maximum reconnect attempts before giving up for the current failure sequence (0 means no retries). Use finite caps for controlled failure handling in automation-sensitive environments.

### `web.reconnect.maxMs`

- Type: `number`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Maximum reconnect backoff cap in milliseconds to bound retry delay growth over repeated failures. Use a reasonable cap so recovery remains timely after prolonged outages.

## Setup Wizard State

Setup wizard state tracking fields that record the most recent guided onboarding run details. Keep these fields for observability and troubleshooting of setup flows across upgrades.

### `wizard`

- Type: `object`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Setup wizard state tracking fields that record the most recent guided onboarding run details. Keep these fields for observability and troubleshooting of setup flows across upgrades.

### `wizard.lastRunAt`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: ISO timestamp for when the setup wizard most recently completed on this host. Use this to confirm onboarding recency during support and operational audits.

### `wizard.lastRunCommand`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Command invocation recorded for the latest wizard run to preserve execution context. Use this to reproduce onboarding steps when verifying setup regressions.

### `wizard.lastRunCommit`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Source commit identifier recorded for the last wizard execution in development builds. Use this to correlate onboarding behavior with exact source state during debugging.

### `wizard.lastRunMode`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: Wizard execution mode recorded as "local" or "remote" for the most recent onboarding flow. Use this to understand whether setup targeted direct local runtime or remote gateway topology.

### `wizard.lastRunVersion`

- Type: `string`
- Required: no
- Default: _none_
- Description: OpenClaw version recorded at the time of the most recent wizard run on this config. Use this when diagnosing behavior differences across version-to-version onboarding changes.
